# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="a823b-102">Veraltete Typen in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a823b-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="a823b-103">In den Tabellen dieses Artikels sind die Typen aufgeführt, die in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] und [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] veraltet sind, geordnet nach Assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a823b-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a823b-104">Über die nachfolgenden Links finden Sie eine Liste der veralteten Typen und empfohlenen Alternativen in den jeweiligen Assemblys.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a823b-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a823b-105">Da diese Typen veraltet sind, sind alle ihrer Member ebenfalls veraltet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a823b-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a823b-106">Eine Liste weiterer veralteter Member in der .NET Framework-Klassenbibliothek finden Sie unter [Veraltete Member](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a823b-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
